Graitec Advance Design 2023
Advance Design was specifically developed for industry professionals that require a superior solution for the structural analysis and design of Reinforced Concrete and Steel structures according to the latest versions of Eurocodes (EC0, EC1, EC2, EC3 and EC8). Advance Design features include easy modeling, a powerful FEM analysis engine, top-level design wizards, automated post-processing of results and automated reports. Achieve a new level of computer-assisted engineering with Advance Design.

Ú©Ø§Ù†Ø§Ù„ Ø¬Ø¯Ø§Ø³Ø§Ø²ÛŒ Ù„Ø±Ø²Ù‡ Ø§ÛŒØŒ Ø³ÛŒØ³ØªÙ… Ù‡Ø§ÛŒ Ù…ÛŒØ±Ø§ÛŒÛŒ (Ù…ÛŒØ±Ø§Ú¯Ø±) Ø§Ù†Ø±Ú˜ÛŒ Ùˆ Ú©Ù†ØªØ±Ù„ Ø§Ø±ØªØ¹Ø§Ø´Ø§Øª
NCREE Taiwan Earthquake Simulation Laboratory
14:02
In reply to this message
The earthquake simulation shaking table in the earthquake simulation laboratory has a total of six degrees of freedom to simulate three-axis earthquakes. At present, major earthquakes in the world can be simulated and reproduced in the earthquake simulation laboratory. The size of the earthquake simulation shaking table is 5 Meter by 5 meters, the mass is 27 metric tons, and the maximum mass of the specimen is 50 metric tons. Its structure is a rectangular structure, making full use of the limited mass to improve its bending moment and torsional stiffness.

The vibrating table is driven by hydraulic actuators, four actuators in each axis, and a total of twelve actuators in three axes. The gravity of the upper specimen is borne by four vertical static supports. The vertical static supports use compressed air to provide bearing capacity. Each bearing has a bearing capacity of 21 metric tons. Air pressure counteracts the gravity of the total moving mass, so that the vertical actuator only needs to provide dynamic force to drive the shaker. The hydraulic pump provides hydraulic power to drive the actuator. Two electric hydraulic pumps and three diesel hydraulic pumps can provide a total flow of 1,325 gpm, and the working pressure of hydraulic oil is 210 kg/cm 2 . The hydraulic pump provides the average flow required by the system, and the difference required for the peak flow is provided by the accumulator. The reaction force required by the actuator to drive the vibrating table is provided by the reaction mass block. About 4,000 metric tons. In order to further improve the quality of the working environment and the experimental environment, the isolation system is used to separate the reaction mass from the fixed foundation. At this time, the reaction mass becomes the floating foundation. The isolation system consists of 96 sets of air springs and 80 Composed of dampers.

Director of the Centre Zhou Zhongzhe
14:06
In reply to this message
Director Zhou Zhongzhe holds a bachelor's degree and a master's degree in the Department of Civil Engineering of National Taiwan University. In 2001, he received a doctorate in structural engineering from the University of California, San Diego (UC San Diego), and then participated in the research and development of the state-of-the-art new San Francisco Oakland Bay by the California Department of Transportation (Caltrans). Bridge (SFOBB) seismic technology. Director Zhou returned to Taiwan in 2003 to teach in the Department of Civil Engineering of Jiaotong University (now Yangming Jiaotong University). From 2012 to 2018, he served as the director of the National Taiwan University Earthquake Engineering Research Center. Established earthquake engineering scholarships to subsidize outstanding doctoral students in the Department of Civil Engineering, and assisted the Construction Department of the Ministry of the Interior to carry out seismic reinforcement design and experiments for 37 new buildings in Banqiao Fuzhou Heyi Residence. In 2017, he served as the National Taiwan University College of Engineering. The vice president assisted in the construction of the Second Industrial Complex, and in 2020, served as the chairman of the Structural Engineering Society of the Republic of China to compile the design specifications for steel-reinforced concrete structures in my country in conjunction with the academic and engineering circles.

ã€€ã€€Director Zhou's research expertise is earthquake engineering, seismic technology research and development of building bridge structures and large-scale structural tests. The research topics include: steel reinforced concrete structures, self-resetting diagonal braces, clip-type buckling beam bracing, steel composite columns and green energy Fan pipe column, high-rise building reinforcement and high-tech workshop earthquake resistance, etc.; in recent years, it has participated in the implementation of the Ministry of Science and Technology, the Ministry of Economic Affairs, the Ministry of Interior Construction Research Institute, the National Transportation Safety Committee, TSMC, Runhong Precision, Foundation Construction, Chunyuan Construction, Donggang Steel Structure, Evergreen Heavy Industries, KGI Commercial Bank, Guande Construction, and Guangyu Construction. He has won the Ministry of Science and Technology Outstanding Young Scholars Program and the Future Technology Award, the Civil and Hydraulic Engineering Society, the Structural Engineering Society, the Steel Structure Association and the Advanced Materials Science and Technology Association, etc. Research Paper Awards, the Ministry of Economic Affairs National Invention and Creation Invention Gold Medal Award, Taipei International Invention and Technology Award The Platinum Award, the highest honor of the Technology Trade Show, the Gold Award Special Award of the Seoul International Invention Exhibition in Korea, the Top Ten Outstanding Inventors in Taiwan and the Lifetime Achievement Award for International Outstanding Inventors, etc. He has published 107 domestic and foreign journals, 173 domestic and foreign seminar articles, 115 book reports, 32 domestic and foreign patents, and 7 R&D technology transfers to domestic and foreign engineering circles.
14:06
In reply to this message
During the severe epidemic in Taiwan, Director Zhou shouldered the heavy responsibility of the director of the center. In addition to cooperating with the centers of the National Academy of Sciences to fight the epidemic, he continued to promote the center's international cooperation and localization of R&D results. Disaster prevention technology is a very important part of the National Earthquake Center. The work will continue to strengthen the cross-disciplinary integration of earthquake science, engineering, and disaster prevention and relief, develop various new earthquake-resistant technologies and automation of construction methods, and enhance the ability of earthquake disaster prevention and early warning of structures near faults in Taiwan to reduce the occurrence of future disasters. The center will also develop intelligent management technology, strengthen the integration of the resources of the two laboratories in the north and the south, improve the efficiency of operation and management, and build a world-class smart laboratory; and further enhance the seismic research and service capacity of energy and key facilities for people's livelihood, and build a domestic green laboratory. The earthquake-resistant test platform for key facilities in the energy and civilian industries serves as a strong backing for the development of Taiwan's sustainable energy industry.
14:08
Experimental support
In order to combine domestic colleges and universities, the National Earthquake Engineering Research Center will effectively utilize the existing experimental resources related to earthquake engineering and enhance its research and development energy. According to the needs of the plan, the National Earthquake Engineering Research Center will dispatch technical personnel and equipment to support each laboratory, and serve the nearby professors and researchers. personnel to conduct relevant earthquake engineering research. Based on the cooperation of each laboratory, the center will further evaluate the reference for setting up the designated service of "cooperative laboratory" in the future.
14:09
test experiment
The Earthquake Simulation Laboratory of the National Earthquake Engineering Research Center has passed ISO 9001, ISO 17025 certification and the evaluation of the laboratory certification system of the Republic of China, and provides standardized and institutionalized testing services. The testing services currently provided include:

Earthquake Simulation Shaker
Long Stroke High Velocity Earthquake Simulation Shaking Table
Reaction walls and strong floors
High Performance Energy Dissipative Component Test System
Multiaxial Test System
Biaxial Dynamic Test System
Fatigue test system
Forced Vibration Test System
Microseismic Measurement System
Comparative Low-Frequency Accelerometer Correction System

MP4 | Video: h264, 1280x720 | Audio: AAC, 44.1 KHz

Structural Design of Shallow type of foundations, in conjuction with STAAD pro software.

What you'll learn
Structural design of concrete foundations
Practical Structural design aspects
Understanding of Design codes and standards pertaining to structural design
Hands on expereince of preparation of Structural design calculations.
Requirements
Basic civil Engineering/Structural Engineering
Basic understanding of STAAD Pro Software
Description
This course in intended to develop professional skills for Engineers who wish to pursue their carrer in Structural Engineering.This course is also valuble for practicing structural engineers ,as a refresher and reference.This course teaches you step by step procedure for Structural Design of foundations.How to use data from STAAD pro software, exporting and utilization in Structural design.Interpreting Geotechnical Reports , to extract Soil parameters for Structural design.Get in depth understanding of Design standards and codes relevant to respective technical clauses.Understaing of concepts of Basic Solid Mechanics behind Structural Engineering.Learn Practical aspects of Structural Design.Examples from Live design Projects.Ready to use downloadable Excel design worsheets are provided as downloadable resources.Finite element approach for design of Raft foundation with STAAD pro software.Local axis convention in STAAD pro for finite elements plates is clearly illustrated and how it different from Local axis of beam element.Importance of direction of forces has been illustraed with diagrams and commentary.Relevant sections from STAAD pro technical reference, have been illustrated for better understanding.Techniques to develop, Stable and Economical Structure.Trouble shooting errors and warnings, occuring while analysis with STAAD Pro software.Providing Stability criteria for foundations and design procedure to ensure Stability of foundations.Optimization solutions for Structural models.

Blast resistancec steel structure design Example:Part 3
Last Updated 05/2022
MP4 | Video: h264, 1280x720 | Audio: AAC, 44.1 KHz, 2 Ch
Genre: eLearning | Language: English + srt | Duration: 8 lectures (2h 9m) | Size: 840.8 MB
thank to senoussiğŸŒ¹
23:40
In reply to this message
Example for steel structure under blast load

What you'll learn
how to design the steel structue under blast load
design for different steel element
apply SDOF and MDOF methods
foundation design under blast load

Requirements
civil or structure engineering knowledge

Description
This course part 3 objective is to present the application of the blast resistance analysis and design for steel structure by a complete example. This course is part 3 as in part 1 is focusing to cover the blast load phenomena and the materials properties values under blast load. This part present also the methods of analyzing the structure under blast load and part2 is the application on example of blast resistance for the concrete structure. In this part 3 presents the case study illustrates the application of blast analysis by using the graph method, the closed formula and also the single degree of freedom (SDOF) by the integration method will be applied. The Newark integration method is illustrated in part1 and in this part3 presents this method and apply it through an excel sheet. These methods for applying structure analysis will be applied for the roof deck, roof purine, wall panel, wall girt and the frame structure and the bracing structure system as usual.

The multi degree of freedom (MDOF) method is also applied for the steel frame by using nonlinear analysis. The foundation design check for blast load will be discuss by checking the overturning, sliding and also design the foundation based on the maximum dynamic load.

Who this course is for
junior and senior structure or civil engineer

TechnoSoft AMETank v14.3.11
12:29
In reply to this message
AMETank enables the rapid configuration, design, and detailing of above-ground shop-built and field-erected storage tanks. Design calculations conform to API 650. Calculations include seismic, internal and external pressures, and wind loading. AMETank supports a fully interactive 3D graphical user interface. The configuration and layout of the tank shell, floor, roof and structure, and subsystems is facilitated through intuitive menus with options customized specifically for tank design. The plates layout and fabrication details are provided. Output for NC machines is supported. Detailed assembly and components fabrication drawings for all substructures, appurtenances, ladders, platforms, stairs, and any other subsystems are supported. A complete design can be configured and detailed in less than two hours including the automatic generation of tank 3D geometry with production details, To-scale drawings, bill of material, and weight & cost reports. Also TechnoSoft provides services for laser scanning and digital reconstruction of tanks, terminals, refineries, and other assets. Assessments include bottom and foundation settlement, shell roundness and verticality, structural column verticality, and floating roof to shell operation. Tank calibration and generation of strapping tables is available. Inspection and integrity analysis services are available. Inspection services include a large array of NDE technologies including ultrasonic, magnetic particle, liquid penetrant, visual, magnetic flux leakage, and vacuum box testing. Tank report calculations on corrosion rates, safe fill height, seismic evaluation, maximum working pressure, and other evaluations as per API 653 are supported.

TechnoSoft AMETank v15.2.16
13:25
In reply to this message
AMETank enables the rapid configuration, design, and detailing of above-ground shop-built and field-erected storage tanks. Design calculations conform to API 650. Calculations include seismic, internal and external pressures, and wind loading. AMETank supports a fully interactive 3D graphical user interface. The configuration and layout of the tank shell, floor, roof and structure, and subsystems is facilitated through intuitive menus with options customized specifically for tank design. The plates layout and fabrication details are provided. Output for NC machines is supported. Detailed assembly and components fabrication drawings for all substructures, appurtenances, ladders, platforms, stairs, and any other subsystems are supported. A complete design can be configured and detailed in less than two hours including the automatic generation of tank 3D geometry with production details, To-scale drawings, bill of material, and weight & cost reports. Also TechnoSoft provides services for laser scanning and digital reconstruction of tanks, terminals, refineries, and other assets. Assessments include bottom and foundation settlement, shell roundness and verticality, structural column verticality, and floating roof to shell operation. Tank calibration and generation of strapping tables is available. Inspection and integrity analysis services are available. Inspection services include a large array of NDE technologies including ultrasonic, magnetic particle, liquid penetrant, visual, magnetic flux leakage, and vacuum box testing. Tank report calculations on corrosion rates, safe fill height, seismic evaluation, maximum working pressure, and other evaluations as per API 653 are supported.

What you'll learn
Our course ensures that you will be able to think with a predictive mindset and understand well the basics of the techniques used in prediction.

Requirements
To get started with Predictive Modelling with Python a solid foundation in statistics is much appreciated. It takes a good amount of understanding to interpret those numbers to understand whether the numbers are adding up or not. Along with the above-mentioned knowledge, one must know to code in Python. Knowing SQL also acts as a complementary skillset. Even if someone is not well equipped with the above-mentioned skill, it should not act as a hindrance as everything is possible with an honest effort and strong will.
Description
It is the use of data and statistics to predict the outcome of the data models. This prediction finds its utility in almost all areas from sports, to TV ratings, corporate earnings, and technological advances. Predictive modeling is also called predictive analytics. With the help of predictive analytics, we can connect data to effective action about the current conditions and future events. Also, we can enable the business to exploit patterns and which are found in historical data to identify potential risks and opportunities before they occur.Python is used for predictive modeling because Python-based frameworks give us results faster and also help in the planning of the next steps based on the results.Our course at EDUCBA is tailor-made for people who are willing to work with a framework that delivers the best result in comparison to the rest of the competitive tools in the market.Our course ensures that you will be able to think with a predictive mindset and understand well the basics of the techniques used in prediction. Critical thinking is very important to validate models and interpret the results. Hence, our course material emphasizes on hardwiring this similar kind of thinking ability.You will have good knowledge about the predictive modeling in python, linear regression, logistic regression, the fitting model with a sci-kit learn library, the fitting model with stat model library, ROC curves, backward elimination approach, stats model package, etc.

6.1 Earthquake Jolts Eastern Afghanistan, 255 Dead

Afghanistan Earthquake: The epicentre was about 44 km from Khost city in Afghanistan and was at a depth of 51 km, said the US Geological Survey (USGS). The European Mediterranean Seismological Centre (EMSC) asserted that people in Pakistan and India also felt tremors.

At least 255 people were killed after an earthquake measuring 6.1 on the richter scale struck eastern Afghanistan early Wednesday. Speaking to reporters, a local government official said that the death toll may rise as several people are seriously injured
The epicentre was about 44 km from Khost city in Afghanistan and was at a depth of 51 km, said the US Geological Survey (USGS). The European Mediterranean Seismological Centre (EMSC) asserted that people in Pakistan and India also felt tremors.

Laminated rubber with tin plug
00:06
In reply to this message
1. Structure and features
Tin (tin) plugged laminated rubber (SnRB) is a damper-integrated seismic isolation support that has the same structure as lead-plugged laminated rubber, and is being promoted to delead industrial products due to its impact on the human body and the environment. Correspondingly, tin is used as a damping material instead of lead.
It has 1.7 times the damping capacity of laminated rubber with lead plugs of the same size, and it is possible to reduce the total number of parts. It also inherits the advantages of lead-plugged laminated rubber, such as space saving, excellent workability, maintainability, and stable performance.

iRDT damper

Inertial spinning top

Inertial Rotary Damping Tube
00:16
In reply to this message
1. Structure and features
This is a device that adds mass by arranging the rotating part of the conventional viscous damping device "RDT (damping top)" on the outside.
The "stretching motion in the axial direction of the device" generated by the deformation of the building is converted into "high-speed rotational motion" by the ball screw mechanism. At this time, the outer cylinder to which the mass is applied generates a large rotational inertia, and the "energy absorption mechanism using a viscous body" driven by it produces a large damping force.

RDT damper

Attenuation device with amplification mechanism-Attenuation top

Rotary Damping Tube
00:20
In reply to this message
1. Structure and features
The damping device with amplification mechanism "Attenuation Top" (RDT) is a damping device consisting of an amplification section that uses a ball screw, which is widely used for industrial machinery, and a damping section that contains a rotating cylinder and fills the gap with a viscous material. ..

The linear motion (axial motion) generated by the interlayer displacement of the building is converted into the rotary motion whose velocity is amplified by the ball screw, and the large damping force is generated by the viscous resistance generated between the outer cylinder of the damping part filled with the viscous body and the rotating body. It is something that demonstrates.

This device has the following features.

â€‹

The amplification mechanism exerts a large damping force even in a small size.

Supports from small-amplitude vibration control to large-amplitude seismic isolation dampers

Less temperature dependent than shear resistance type viscous dampers

Easy to install and suitable for seismic retrofitting of existing buildings

CLB

Linear rolling bearings

Cross Linear Bearing
00:21
In reply to this message
1. Structure and features
The linear motion rolling bearing (CLB) is a bearing that slides in any direction by combining a linear motion device (LM guide) consisting of a steel block with a steel ball circulation mechanism and a bearing rail in a cross shape.
There are three types, cross-shaped (1 piece), key-shaped (2 pieces), and well-shaped (4 pieces), depending on the number of blocks used for one set of bearings.
This bearing has the following features.
1 Extremely low horizontal resistance makes it possible to extend the period of seismic isolated buildings
2 Can be applied to lightweight buildings and improves design freedom
3 Effective for pulling forces and can be applied to tower-shaped buildings
4 Almost horizontal rigidity Effective for eccentric balance control of irregular buildings because it can support the load without adding it.
5 Wide selection of device sizes, wide range from floor seismic isolation and small houses to heavy-duty super high-rise buildings
6 Depending on the length of the rail The movable length can be set freely (maximum value of limit deformation = Â± 1000 mm)
7 Performance does not depend on temperature or speed
Since this bearing does not have a restoration function or a seismic isolation function, it is usually combined with a laminated rubber bearing with a lead plug. To use.

VDW

Viscous Damping Wall

Ù…ÛŒØ±Ø§Ú¯Ø± Ø¯ÛŒÙˆØ§Ø± Ø¨Ø±Ø´ÛŒ ÙˆÛŒØ³Ú©ÙˆØ²
00:26
In reply to this message
1. Structure and features
The viscous damping wall is a damping device that utilizes the viscous resistance of a highly viscous fluid. A container in which a multi-layered steel plate forms a thin box is filled with a highly viscous viscous material, and the steel plate is inserted through the opening at the top.

Due to vibration, shear resistance is generated when the steel plate suspended from above moves inside the viscous body, suppressing shaking.

â€‹

This viscous damping wall has the following features.

1 Supports not only earthquake motion but also various vibrations such as wind vibration and mechanical vibration.

Supports both horizontal and vertical deformation in two planes

3 Highly durable and reliable, no need to replace viscous material

4 Can be manufactured in any size and has a high degree of design freedom

5 Can be installed in any location such as core and partition

6 Effective against tower cranes under construction and vibration caused by wind, improving construction accuracy and safety.
00:26
In reply to this message

Viscous Damping Wall mini

1. Structure and features
VDWmini (Viscous Damping Wall mini, small multi-layer viscous damping wall) is a compact size of about 1m square with good installability by multiplying the inner wall steel plate of the viscous damping wall into 4 or 6 layers to increase the effective area. It is a shear resistance type viscous vibration control device that enables you to obtain performance. It is composed of an inner wall steel plate connected to the upper floor side and an outer wall steel plate connected to the lower floor side, and polyisobutylene, which has almost no deterioration over time, is used for the highly viscous fluid inside.

â€‹

This device has the following features.

â€‹

1 This device exerts a viscous resistance force that depends on the operating speed, and has the characteristic that the change due to the speed is large in the low speed range, and the change becomes gradual as the speed increases.

2 Since the dependence on the frequency is small, resistance can be expected in the same way in structures with various periodic characteristics.

3 It has the characteristics that the resistance decreases as the temperature rises and the resistance increases as the temperature decreases.

4 With respect to repeated vibration for a long time, the resistance decreases as the temperature of the viscous fluid rises, but it has the property of returning to its original performance as the temperature drops over time.

ØªØ§ÛŒÛŒØ¯Ù‡ Ø³ÛŒØ³ØªÙ… Ú©Ù†ØªØ±Ù„ Ú©ÛŒÙÛŒØª ØªÙˆÙ„ÛŒØ¯ Ø¬Ø¯Ø§Ø³Ø§Ø² Ø§Ù„Ø§Ø³ØªÙˆÙ…Ø±ÛŒ Ø¨Ø§ Ù‡Ø³ØªÙ‡ Ù‚Ù„Ø¹ÛŒ ØªÙˆÙ„ÛŒØ¯ Ø´Ø±Ú©Øª ADC Ø¯Ø± 2021 ØªÙˆØ³Ø· Ù…Ø±Ú©Ø² ØªØ­Ù‚ÛŒÙ‚Ø§Øª Ø³Ø§Ø®ØªÙ…Ø§Ù† Ú˜Ø§Ù¾Ù†
00:49
Japan's first seismic isolation structure
In Japan, half a year before the 1891 Nobi earthquake (M8.4), a lecture entitled "Structure that does not receive large vibrations during an earthquake" when logs are laid out in two directions and a building is built on top of them. Was performed by architect Kozo Kawai, and the speed record remains.

There is no clear record, but it seems that John Milne, a former miner who stayed in Japan from 1876 to 1994 and the father of Japanese seismic science, built at least two seismic isolated buildings, which is the first seismic isolation in Japan. It is thought to be a seismic structure. Cast iron balls were sandwiched under the pillars at the four corners of the wooden building, and it seems that the slow movement of the earthquake was transmitted, but the sudden movement was not transmitted.

Image: Kawai Kozo (1985-1934)
Source-Published by Architectural Institute of Japan, "Architectural Magazine November 1934"
00:50
Birth of seismic design method
The 1906 San Francisco earthquake (M8.3) triggered the development of modern seismic structures, and Dr. Fusakichi Omori (seismology) and Dr. Riki Sano (building structure) conducted field surveys from Japan.

Riki Sano reports that ramen-type steel structures and reinforced concrete structures are excellent in terms of earthquake resistance. In 1915, Sano published "House Seismic Structure Theory" and proposed "Seismic Intensity Method" as a seismic design method.

Following the Great Kanto Earthquake (M7.9) of 1923, in 1924, the "horizontal seismic intensity 0.1" was incorporated into the Urban Building Law, and the world's first seismic design method was born.
00:50
In reply to this message
After the Great Kanto Earthquake, many seismic isolation structures have been proposed by architectural structure researchers such as Kensaburo Kito, Koya Yamashita, Taro Nakamura, and Ryuichi Oka. In principle, most of the current seismic isolation and damping structures were proposed, but at that time, before World War II, only Ryuichi Oka actually built them.

â€‹

Image : Riki Sano (1880-1956)
Source-Published by the Architectural Institute of Japan, "Architectural Magazine December 1956"
00:50
Rigid or flexible structure
Around 1930 in the early Showa period, there was a "flexible debate" about whether a rigid structure was good or a flexible structure, and Kensaburo Mashima of the Navy who insisted on a flexible structure called "seismic house structure", which is a flexible story. Is proposing. However, in the situation where basic data on the earthquake motion itself is insufficient, the rigid structure becomes mainstream without the end of the controversy being clear, and it enters World War II.



Image: Former Ryogoku Kokugikan that was devastated by the Great Kanto Earthquake
Source-Collection of Sumida Ward Library "Kokugikan"
00:50
From seismic design method to new seismic design method
In 1944, before the end of the war, a seismic design method based on ultimate strength was temporarily enacted to save materials. Taking over that idea, the allowable stress of the material was doubled when the Building Standards Act was enacted in 1950, and the design horizontal seismic intensity was raised from 0.1 to 0.2 accordingly. At this time, the idea of short-term and long-term is introduced into structural design.

Before the war, most of the buildings were low-rise, with many walls and high rigidity, but after the war, the number of buildings with large openings and low rigidity will increase. As a result, in medium- and low-rise buildings, the shaking during an earthquake is amplified to two to three times the shaking of the ground, but the era of static design horizontal seismic intensity 0.2 will continue for a long time.



Image: 1933 Ginza
Source-Hakubunkan "Great Tokyo Photo Guide"
00:51
Enforcement of new seismic design law
After the Great Kanto Earthquake, the North Tango Earthquake (1927, M7.5), Sanriku (1933, M8.3), Tottori (1943, M7.4), Tonankai (1944, M8.0), Nankai (1944, M8.0) The 1946, M8.1) and 1948 Fukui earthquakes (M7.8) and other major earthquakes occurred in succession, but for the next half century, no severe earthquakes occurred near the metropolitan areas.

The Tokachi-oki Earthquake (M7.9) that occurred in 1968 severely damaged a reinforced concrete building designed based on the Building Standards Law, and the design standards of the Architectural Institute of Japan were revised. Incorporating the results of various seismic studies since then, the Building Standards Law was amended in 1981, and the current "New Seismic Design Law" is now in force.
00:51
In reply to this message
The "new seismic design method" adopts the "two-step design method". The first stage aims at "no damage to the building" for moderate earthquakes that may be encountered during the life of the building, and the second stage is for very strong ground motions such as the Great Kanto Earthquake. Our goal is to prevent the collapse of buildings, with the first priority being to secure human life.


Image: Daiwa Department Store immediately after the Fukui Earthquake
Source-Mainichi Newspaper "Sun Photo Newspaper (June 30, 1948 edition)"
00:51
Legal development for the spread of seismic isolation and damping structures
The seismic structure entrusts all of the two functions of "load support of the building" and "absorption of seismic energy input to the building" to the building structure.

On the other hand, the seismic isolation structure is intended to "absorb the input energy of an earthquake with a seismic isolation device and release columns and beams from the role of energy absorption."

In addition, the seismic control structure is intended to "quickly consume the seismic energy input to the building with a powerful energy absorbing device (vibration control device) to eliminate the need for energy absorption by columns and beams."
00:51
In reply to this message
The seismic isolation structure has expanded rapidly since the Great Hanshin-Awaji Earthquake in 1995. Many used laminated rubber seismic isolation devices that were put into practical use in New Zealand. At that time, in order to construct a seismic isolated structure, it was necessary to obtain the evaluation of the Building Center of Japan and the approval of the Minister of Construction, and it took about 3 months to clear these.

After that, various types of seismic isolation devices will be developed and put into practical use. As a result, by using a seismic isolation device (certified seismic isolation member) certified for the purpose of popularizing seismic isolation structures from April 2001, if certain conditions are met, no rating or ministerial approval is required, and it is normal. It is now possible to construct a seismic isolated building by following the building confirmation procedure.

â€‹

Image: Great Hanshin-Awaji Earthquake (in front of Nishimura Coffee in Nakayamatedori)
Author-Akiyoshi Matsuoka ( Creative Commons )
00:52
Maintaining the function of the building
In the 2011 off the Pacific coast of Tohoku Earthquake (M9.0) that occurred on March 11, 2011, there were many seismic isolated and controlled buildings in the disaster area. Among them, there were a few that had minor damage to the damping device and the surrounding area, but the seismic isolation function was maintained even in the aftershock, and the effect was fully demonstrated.
00:52
In reply to this message
Seismic isolation structures are used in various applications such as government offices, hospitals, schools, offices, and apartment buildings. What was found this time is not only to maintain the soundness of the building but also to secure energy and communication means in order for the seismic isolated / damping building to continue to maintain its function / role in an environment where the infrastructure is disrupted. Furthermore, as a building that should play a role as a regional disaster prevention base, it was necessary to stockpile chemicals, food, cold protection equipment, temporary toilets, etc.

â€‹

Image : Seismic isolated condominium in Sendai City that encountered the 2011 off the Pacific coast of Tohoku Earthquake
00:52
Measures against long-period ground motion
In this earthquake, a skyscraper with a long natural period continued to shake greatly for a long time. It is reported that the skyscrapers in Shinjuku continued to shake up to over 1 meter for 13 minutes.

It was a skyscraper that was said to be strong against earthquakes, but the building shook greatly because it resonated with the long-period component of seismic motion. The possibility of such a phenomenon has been pointed out, but the countermeasures for relatively old skyscrapers are not sufficient.
00:52
In reply to this message
In the future, not only newly planned skyscrapers, but also existing skyscrapers, it is desired to take measures to reduce shaking against long-period ground motion by "vibration control repair" by adding damping devices.

â€‹

Image : Skyscrapers in Shinjuku
00:53
It seems to be a human instinct to want to escape from the shaking of an earthquake, and there is a story that a person named Zhang Heng made a seismograph in the late Han era (around 136) in China.

According to Professor Cary of the University of California, in 1909 the British doctor Callantariant laid a stone called talc under the building and proposed a method to insulate the building from the ground, which is the world's first seismic isolation structure. ..

Meanwhile, Professor Buckle of New York State University told German Jacob Bektord how to dig a hole in the ground, put a ball in it and build a building on it, one month after the 1906 San Francisco earthquake. I have found that I have applied for a patent in the United States.

Ideal damping is a viscous damping mechanism
ãƒ» The most effective damping mechanism for suppressing the dynamic vibration of a structure is viscous damping.
ãƒ»
Viscous damping allows the response acceleration to be smoothly and effectively suppressed without increasing the resistance of the entire structure because the resistance is proportional to the velocity.
ãƒ»
Dynamic design has solved the problem of achieving a large viscous damping force with high reliability up to the large amplitude range.

BP-CAP for cast-in-place piles!

This device enables "complete pin joining of pile heads", dramatically reducing the stress during earthquakes generated at the pile heads and the stress on foundations and underground beams, improving seismic performance and excellent workability and economic efficiency. It is possible to realize a basic structure.

In reply to this message
What is the seismic problem in the middle of the pile?
ã€€ãƒ»
In the part where the stratum composition changes suddenly, the degree of shear strain of the stratum at the time of an earthquake changes suddenly, so that the pile is subjected to forced deformation of the stratum, and large bending stress and shear stress are locally generated.
02:23
Dynamic design pile cover method solves this problem
ã€€ãƒ»
In order to resolve the local seismic stress in the middle of the pile, it is necessary to alleviate the local curvature of the pile caused by the forced displacement of the formation.
ã€€ãƒ»
In the pile cover method, a soft soft cover layer is provided on the surface of the pile body, and the deformation of this cover layer smoothly relaxes the local curvature of the pile and reduces the stress generated in the pile during an earthquake.

â–  Recommendation of seismic isolated building (by Dynamic Design Inc, in Japanese)

Why Dynamic recommends seismic isolation

Dynamic Design is a structural design office that specializes in seismic isolation and damping structures.
Why does Dynamic recommend a seismic isolation structure?
Why not design a conventional structural building? And what kind of seismic isolation does Dynamic design?
We think about architectural design:

1. 1. What is seismic design?

I think it is "designing a building that is safe against a large earthquake." Even if the building does not collapse, if the hospital becomes useless immediately after the earthquake or if the life in the condominium is paralyzed, I think that the seismic design is a failure.

2. 2. What is building safety?

It is not enough that the building does not collapse due to the earthquake.
ãƒ» No one will be injured as well as dead.
ãƒ» The function is maintained and it can be used immediately after an earthquake.
ãƒ» Furniture should not fall over or equipment should not be damaged, and both the contents and secondary parts should be sound.
ãƒ» The asset value is preserved without the need for repairs.
Buildings that are safe against earthquakes can achieve these goals.

3. 3. The actual seismic motion is

It turns out to be very strict and strong.
In both the Hyogoken Nanbu Earthquake and the Northridge Earthquake in the United States, which trashed 20 million tons of structures, seismic motions with a maximum acceleration of 800 to 1000 gals and a maximum velocity of 90 to 100 cm / s or more were recorded. It is not easy to design a building safely against such a strong earthquake motion.
02:30
Scars of the Great Hanshin Earthquake in 1995
02:31
4. Mid-to-low-rise buildings can only be saved by seismic isolation

Most of the buildings in Japan are low-rise buildings with 10 or more floors or less, and are short-period structures with a period of 1 second or less. The maximum response acceleration of short-period structures is amplified to 2 to 3 times that of the ground motion. It is not possible to seismically design a general building against seismic forces whose base shear coefficient greatly exceeds 1.0.
However, if a seismic isolation structure is adopted, the base shear coefficient can be increased.
It can be suppressed to around 0.2, and the difficult seismic design becomes realistic for the first time. Seismic isolation can save low-rise buildings that are exposed to the most severe seismic response. However, the name seismic isolation does not mean that everything is safe. The safety of the seismic isolated building also depends on the design.

5. What kind of seismic isolation is aimed at

The strength of the seismic motion does not change depending on the importance of the structure and the design content, much less it does not match the market price of the design. If the actual ground motion is much more severe than the design market, I think it should change the setting of the design ground motion.
December 1995 Dynamic Design designed "Meidaimae Mansion" which is undamaged against earthquake motion with maximum input degree Vmax = 100cm / s. In November 1996, we achieved the first building (Fig. 1) of the highest seismic performance rank "C4-A" in the new rating system.
Dynamic design always aims for the highest safety performance as long as the design conditions allow. By thoroughly pursuing performance, we believe that we can realize a building that is economically advantageous and has excellent architectural space and functions.
We hope to contribute to the realization of attractive seismic isolated buildings with ingenuity and passion in order to build a safe and prosperous city and social capital in harmony with the natural environment.
02:31
C4-A achievement first building
02:31
â–  Challenge to earthquakes: History of earthquake resistance, seismic isolation, and vibration control structure -Part 1-

-History of development of seismic isolation structure seen overseas and in Japan-

"I want to minimize the damage caused by earthquakes" This has been a major problem since the dawn of history for people living in earthquake-prone areas.
The seismic isolation structure and vibration control structure, which have been attracting attention since the Great Hanshin-Awaji Earthquake, can be seen to have developed at the same time as the seismic construction method by tracing its history.


Seismic design method born from the San Francisco earthquake

Human challenges to earthquakes can be traced back to the story of a person named Zhang Heng who had already made a seismograph in the late Han era (136). However, it was the 1906 San Francisco Earthquake (M8.3) that triggered the development of modern seismic structures. From Japan, Dr. Fusakichi Omori (Seismology) and Riki Sano (Architectural Structure) conducted a field survey, and Sano reported that ramen-type steel structures and reinforced concrete structures are superior in terms of earthquake resistance. In 1915, he published the theory of seismic structure of houses, in which he proposed the "seismic intensity method" as a seismic design method. After that, in the wake of the Great Kanto Earthquake (M7.9) in 1923, the following year, "Horizontal Seismic Intensity 0.1 was incorporated into the Urban Building Law", and the world's first seismic design regulations were born.

Seismic isolation design method that insulates the building from the ground with talc and boulders

The idea of â€‹â€‹separating the building from the ground seems to have been around for a long time. Professor Kelly of the University of California said that "a method of laying a stone called talc under the building to insulate the building from the ground" (upper right figure) proposed by the British doctor Calantarian in 1909 is the world's first proposal for a seismic isolation structure. is.
Meanwhile, Professor Buckle of New York State University suggested that German Jacob Bektord "how to dig a hole in the ground, put a ball and build a building on it," just one month after the San Francisco earthquake (May 1906). I found that I applied for a patent in the United States.
02:31
Seismic isolation construction method with logs lined up

In Japan, about half a year before the 1891 Nobi Earthquake (M8.4), Kawai was entitled "Great Earthquake Earthquake Receiving Structure" in which logs were laid out in two directions and a building was built on top of them. Kozo's speech speed record has been discovered by Yuji Ohashi (Building Research Institute, Ministry of Construction).
However, in a letter to a friend by Callantarian, "My invention is better than the Japanese seismic isolation structure proposed 25 years ago (around 1884)", and Kawai's proposal to Japan. It means that there was already a seismic isolation structure before. It was unknown for a long time what kind of seismic isolation structure, but Mitsuo Miyazaki (Dynamic Design) discovered a clue to clarify it.

Bearing construction method in front of the log

The Meiji government has invited 2,000 and 5,000 "hired foreigners" from Europe and the United States. Among them is John Milne, a former mining engineer and father of Japanese seismology. He founded the world's first Seismological Society of Japan, and while conducting extensive research on earthquakes such as making seismographs, past records, and field surveys, he seems to have built at least two seismic isolated buildings. By sandwiching a cast iron ball under the pillars at the four corners of a wooden building, the slow movement of the earthquake was transmitted, but the sudden movement was not transmitted. The seismic isolation structure of Japan, which was known to the United Kingdom, belongs to Milne because his stay in Japan was from 1876 to 1994 and he sent many papers and reports to Europe including the United Kingdom. That seems almost certain.

Going back in time, Hikone Castle was said to be "during the earthquake." In addition, the five-storied pagoda may be said to be a kind of seismic control structure composed of a pillar and many wooden structures.
02:32
â–  Challenge to earthquakes: History of earthquake resistance, seismic isolation, and vibration control structure -Part 2-

-History of the development of seismic isolation structures seen overseas and in Japan Part 2-

The seismic isolation structure that began to be proposed after the Great San Francisco Earthquake has been proposed one after another in the wake of the Great Kanto Earthquake, and some have actually been constructed. This time, I would like to introduce the challenge of seismic isolation structure before World War II.


Seismic isolation structure of the former Imperial Hotel with soft strata as cushions

When American genius architect Frank Loyd Wright was designing the former Imperial Hotel in Tokyo (1921), the thickness of the site was that he had 60 to 70 feet of soft strata beneath 8 feet of surface. Turned out. "Why not float the building!", He considers this soft stratum to be a heavenly blessing that absorbs the impact of the earthquake, and is said to have designed a pile foundation that looks like a floating structure by overcoming the opposition of the surroundings. .. Two years after the building was completed (1923), I encountered the Great Kanto Earthquake, but the building survived the earthquake.

Seismic isolation structure in the United States after the San Francisco earthquake

After proposing seismic isolation structures for Jacob Bectold and Callantarian, Martel proposed "Flexble First Story" in 1929 in the United States. The concept is to make the first floor of the building softer than the other parts, and to soften the impact force of the earthquake there, and after the research of Green (1935) and Jacobsen (1938), the concept of energy absorption by plasticization. Developed into "The Soft first Story Method" (1969, Fintel & Kahn). The first Olive View hospital using this method will be built in the suburbs of Los Angeles. The hospital, which has just been completed, was severely damaged by the San Fernando earthquake in 1971. At present, it is interpreted that it is impossible to absorb the input energy of the entire building with only one layer of columns made of brittle material such as reinforced concrete, and the piloti type should be avoided even in Japan's new seismic design method. Is now required.
02:32
Challenge to seismic isolation structure after the Great Kanto Earthquake

With the Great Kanto Earthquake, which killed 140,000 people, many seismic isolation structures have been proposed one after another, saying "I want to escape from the earthquake disaster." In the year following the earthquake, Kensaburo Kito's ball bearing proposal and Koya Yamashita's proposal for spring-loaded columns, Taro Nakamura's pin columns + pump-type dampers (1927), Ryuichi Oka (1928) and Kenzaburo Mashima (1934) There are suggestions and so on. Around 1930 in the early Showa period, there was a famous "soft and rigid controversy" between Sano and Muto vs. Mashima about whether the rigid structure was good or the flexible structure was good.
Mashima, who insisted on a flexible structure, proposed a seismic isolation structure that combines his Flexible First Story proposed by Martel in the United States with a one-story building that plays the role of fail-safe in the "seismic house structure". It seems that information exchange was quite active at that time as well.
Of the many seismic isolation structures proposed in the wake of the Great Kanto Earthquake, only the one proposed by Ryuichi Oka in 1933 was actually realized.

Seismic isolation pillar by Ryuichi Oka

Ryuichi Oka's proposal for "seismic isolation foundation" is to install a seismic isolation pillar with a large spherical bottom and use a spherical pin joint at the upper end. It is a mechanism that allows horizontal displacement. In addition, it also has a damping (energy absorption) function due to the friction of the rotating part. The Fudo Savings Bank (*) Himeji Branch and Shimonoseki Branch, which were built in 1934 by applying this mechanism, are said to be the world's first existing practical seismic isolated buildings.
*) The current Asahi Bank, the former Kyowa Bank, and the Fudo Bank at that time are still in use today, but it seems that the seismic isolation mechanism of the Himeji branch has already lost its function. However, when standing in front of this seismic isolated pillar, the passion and romance of our ancestors who realized their passion for seismic isolation as an actual structure are still transmitted to us.
02:32
â–  Challenge to earthquakes: History of earthquake resistance, seismic isolation, and vibration control structure -Part 3-

History of development of seismic isolation structure seen overseas and in Japan Part 3

Around 1970, the challenge to earthquakes took a step from the research stage to the practical stage, and actual seismic isolation structures began to be constructed little by little around the world.

Skopje Seismic Isolation Elementary School

Skopje, the capital of the Republic of Macedonia, suffered catastrophic damage in the 1963 earthquake, with about half of his 50,000 buildings collapsed and more than 80% of the damage. Disaster recovery assistance is provided from various countries centered on UNESCO, and in 1969, with the assistance of Switzerland, the Heinrich Pestaroch Elementary School, the world's first seismic isolated building that adopted rubber bearings for earthquake countermeasures, will be completed. The seismic isolation device used in a relatively small school building with a wall-type RC structure on three floors is a mass of rubber made by laminating five square rubber plates with a thickness of 7 cm and a side of 70 cm, which is about 50 tons. It swells as shown in the photo due to the load. This handmade isolator, elaborate foundation for creep countermeasures, and foam glass blocks for restraining wind sway that have already been covered with moss convey the passion of engineers who worked on three-dimensional seismic isolation as the world's first challenge.

New Zealand Seismic Isolation Bridge

"South Rangitikei Viaduct" was started in 1974 and pioneered the seismic isolation of New Zealand. A 315m long concrete railroad bridge crosses 80m above the plain, where sheep and cows flock, and its green valley. This bridge, which is sandwiched between rocks on both banks, converts the motion in the direction perpendicular to the bridge axis into the vertical stepping motion of the two piers, and the twist deformation of the steel "Torsion Beam" charged in the piers. It is a mechanism that absorbs energy and is called "Stepping Structure". A brave figure in harmony with nature encourages us to create creative activities full of creativity.

New Zealand seismic isolated building

In 1981, New Zealand completed the "William Clayton Building," which was the first in the world to use laminated rubber with lead plugs, and had a global impact on the practical application of seismic isolated buildings.
Two years later, he completed the 12-story "Union House" building. This building is located on the coast of Auckland, where the ground conditions are not very good. A seismic isolated building with a period of about 2 seconds has been realized by using a support pile with a depth of about 13 m as a flexible pile with a double pipe structure. The upper structure has a brace placed on the outer circumference to increase the rigidity, and a steel history damper is placed between the lower end of the upper structure and the ground side fixing part. This method is the seismic isolation structure itself proposed by Taro Nakamura in 1927 after the Kanto earthquake.
In 1990, the 10-story seismic isolation building "Wellington Central" combined this flexible pile with the cylinder type lead damper "Lead Extrusion Damper".
The Police Station "has been completed.
02:33
Seismic isolation building in the United States

The first seismic isolation structure in the United States is a power barrier completed in 1979. Some of the young researchers who have worked to realize seismic isolation structures in New Zealand moved to the United States, and in the 1980s, the momentum for realizing seismic isolation buildings in California rapidly increased. However, due to the conservative environment of the litigation society, the first seismic isolated building "Foothill communities Law & Justice Center" was completed in 1986. In contrast to the rapid spread of seismic isolated buildings in Japan, which coincided with the bubble economy, very few seismic isolated buildings were realized in the latter half of the 1980s. However, with the 1989 Loma Prieta earthquake and the 1994 Northridge earthquake as tailwinds, seismic isolation in the United States is steadily spreading in both bridges and construction.
In the United States, seismic isolation is adopted from socially important public buildings such as government buildings, hospitals, fire departments, and courts, and there are many cases of seismic isolation retrofit to improve the seismic performance of historic buildings. Excellent seismic isolation buildings are being realized, and efforts that should be referred to in Japan are being made.

â–  Seismic isolation building's seismic performance-Seismic isolation hospital that was hit by a direct earthquake-

The goal of the seismic isolation structure is to "protect both the building and its contents without damage against a large earthquake." Is there a successful example of achieving this goal in an actual earthquake?
The North Ridge Earthquake that occurred in the San Fernando Valley in the United States before dawn on January 17, 1994 had a magnitude of M = 6.7, which was a medium-sized earthquake, but in an instant, more than 7,000 people were injured. In this emergency, the "conventional seismic structure hospital" lost its hospital function, and the "seismic isolation structure hospital" fulfilled its mission without any damage.

1. 1. Strength of seismic motion

The maximum acceleration of the ground motion in the center of Los Angeles reaches about 0.25G to 0.50G, and the horizontal 1.82G and vertical 1.18G on the ground (epicentral distance 7km) in the San Fernando Valley area, which is closer to the epicenter, is the Olive View Hospital (epicentral distance). Acceleration of 0.91G horizontally and 0.60G vertically is recorded on the ground of the site (distance 15km). (CSMIP Report)

2. 2. At that time, at the "conventional seismic structure hospital"

Oliveview Hospital was severely damaged by the 1971 San Fernando earthquake and collapsed, so the site was relocated and rebuilt 10 years later. A 6-story hospital with earthquake-resistant walls arranged in the 10 o'clock shape of the hospital mark, the maximum horizontal acceleration on the first floor
0.82G was input, and the maximum acceleration of the rooftop floor reached "2.31G". The structural skeleton withstood this seismic force of 1G or more well, and escaped collapse to the extent that a crack occurred in the shear wall. However, the medical equipment and furniture inside fell, documents such as medical records fell and scattered, and the sprinkler piping broke and flooded all floors, making the building unusable and evacuating the entire building.
The hospital will transfer all 300 inpatients to another facility by 7:00 pm on the same day, and will resume some inpatient treatment services 41 hours on January 19, his third day after the earthquake. However, during this period, only outdoor first aid services have been provided for a long time.

3. 3. At that time, at the "Seismic Isolation Hospital"
02:33
About 5 km northeast of downtown Los Angeles, there is a major medical center at a university hospital called the USC Medical Center. Among them was his 8-story seismic isolation hospital, which was the only one in the world at that time called "USC Seismic Isolation Hospital". The maximum horizontal acceleration of 0.49G on the surface of the site and 0.37G directly under the seismic isolation device was received, but the maximum acceleration of the building was 0.21G on the roof and only 0.10G to 0.15G on the 1st to 7th floors. It was demonstrated wonderfully.
The ward is lined with shelves 6 to 8 feet high, but none of the vases and bottles fell during the mainshock and subsequent aftershocks, and there were abnormalities in the OA equipment and other equipment on the desk. There was no damage, and the hospital function was completely undamaged and undamaged.
At 4:31 am when the earthquake struck, emergency brain surgery was about to take place in the ward. An earthquake occurred when a scalpel was about to be inserted. The surgery was started immediately after the gentle shaking subsided in less than a minute, and the surgery was completed without delay (D.R.Edens USC Hospital).
This building with a total floor area of â€‹â€‹30,000 m2 is supported by 68 lead-plugged laminated rubber (LRB) and 81 laminated rubber (RB), for a total of 149 seismic isolation devices.
Many drug bottles fell in his 4-story drug building adjacent to this seismic isolated ward. It is also reported that one wing of the main ward for inpatient treatment was temporarily closed due to aftershocks, and the total damage to the "conventional seismic structure" building in the center reached $ 350mil (about 38.5 billion yen at that time). increase.

â–  Design concept of seismic isolation / damping structure 1 -Issues of seismic design and seismic isolation strategy-

The Great Hanshin Earthquake produced 6,000 dead, 10 trillion yen in economic loss, and 20 million tons of waste in just 10 seconds. We will return to the origin of "what should be seismic design" including seismic isolation and damping structure, and reconsider the design concept.

1. 1. The essence of the current seismic design concept

The new seismic design method (Building Standards Law) is
1. Almost no damage to seismic motion with a seismic intensity of 4 to 5 lower.
2. Prevention of collapse against strong earthquake motion with seismic intensity of 5 or higher
Is the design goal. The aim is to achieve the long-cherished desire of not wanting to lose only human life even in a large earthquake.
Increases the toughness of structural members as well as strength to avoid collapse. It is designed so that the seismic energy input to the building is uniformly absorbed throughout the building as historical energy due to plastic deformation of each part.
However, the condition of simultaneous yielding of each layer is not easily satisfied, and energy is concentrated in a specific layer. Plasticization of structural members means damage, and the more energy absorbed, the more damaged and dangerous the building becomes.
Energy absorption to avoid damage cannot be achieved without damage. It is a tactic that is prepared to die by cutting meat and not cutting bones.

2. 2. Challenges and distress of seismic design

Would it be a pleasure if the building did not collapse and the design goals were achieved?
Nine hospitals lost their functions in the Northridge earthquake, although no hospitals collapsed. In the Great Hanshin Earthquake, the condominiums that took their lives were full of scratches, and the only thing that was unharmed was the loan. Although the pillars and beams are okay, is it possible to repair a building whose miscellaneous walls and partition walls have been sheared and broken and live comfortably? If furniture and equipment fall and scatter, your home or office will be messed up. The elevator did not move, and the equipment and equipment lost their functions. If the supply of water, electricity and gas is cut off and drainage becomes impossible, even the toilet cannot be used.
Life after an earthquake is paralyzed, asset values â€‹â€‹are lost, and the economic base collapses. Unfortunately, these problems remain unsolved in the design concept of collapse prevention.
Then, if the building is made sturdy anyway, the building will shake more and more, the risk of the contents falling or falling will increase, and it will become more difficult to ensure the safety of equipment. No matter how hard the designer struggles, the problem is not easily solved.
02:38
3. 3. Severe reality of earthquake motion

In reality, a seismic intensity of 7 occurred and a maximum acceleration of around 1000 gal was recorded, and it has become clear that the actual seismic motion is extremely severe. Most of the buildings in the world are low-rise buildings with a cycle of 1 second or less. The shaking of short-period structures is amplified to 2 to 3 times the input seismic motion. In other words, 10 times the current design seismic force acts on the building. With this, the design of a normal building cannot be established, and it is a waste to consider ensuring the safety of the equipment and contents inside the building.
02:39
Seismic isolation structure
02:39
Conventional structure
02:39
4. Seismic isolation structure strategy

The seismic isolation structure solves this difficult problem with the following approach. First, a seismic isolation layer with extremely low rigidity compared to each layer of the upper building is constructed, and all deformation and energy are concentrated here. The seismic isolation device absorbs all of the seismic energy input to the building, freeing the upper building from energy damage. The resistance of the seismic isolation device is kept constant, and no more force is applied to the upper building. As a result, the entire building becomes one mass, and all floors have the same shaking. The idea is to turn violent vibrations into gentle vibrations and protect both the building and its contents intact. The key to the safety of a seismic isolated building is how large the seismic isolation device can deform horizontally while supporting the weight of the building.
At present, the shaking of the building can be suppressed to about 200 gal, which is about 1/5 to 1/10 of the conventional structure, against the strong input of 500 to 1000 gal at the time of a big earthquake.
Only by adopting a seismic isolation structure can the building be designed undamaged against a large earthquake, and the contents and equipment can be safely protected.

Issues and directions of seismic isolation / damping architecture

What kind of progress will the seismic isolation / damping structure, which has been gradually realized since the 1980s in advanced seismic engineering countries such as NZ, the United States, and Japan, with the emergence of pioneering attempts in the 1970s? It's a fun task.
This time, let's consider the future direction of seismic isolation structures and seismic control structures centered on high-rise buildings, whose examples are rapidly increasing.

1. 1. Two directions of seismic isolated building

The trend of seismic isolated buildings, which is rapidly becoming widespread, currently has two completely different directions.
One is an effort to realize a safer structure as the actual situation of severe earthquake motion is clarified. We are aiming for a seismic isolated building that is safe even for seismic motions that exceed the conventional design seismic motion level Vmax = 50 cm / s and are stronger than Vmax = 100 cm / s or higher. In the Northridge Earthquake and the Great Hanshin Earthquake, severe seismic motion of around Vmax = 100 cm / s is actually recorded. It was
The other is a move to aim for a popular version of seismic isolated building with the catchphrase "seismic isolated building at the same cost as the conventional construction method". The strategy is to use seismic isolation devices at the lowest possible cost, with the design goal of seismic motion of Vmax = 50 cm / s as before, and to survive the oversupplied condominium market with "seismic isolation = sold out".
The current rapid growth of seismic isolated buildings (Fig. 1) includes various movements in between, but due to the ideas of designers and building planners, these two directions will continue in the future. Is expected.

Dynamic design wants to be the flag bearer of the former. Economic efficiency is an important issue, but we should not aim to reduce the cost of seismic isolated buildings by lowering the specifications of seismic isolation devices or lowering the level of input seismic motion. The cost destruction of seismic isolation devices is imminent.
Safety up does not necessarily mean cost up, and there is a way to realize economically advantageous seismic isolation construction by thoroughly pursuing safety. We believe that it is the role of dynamic design to present the solution.
02:41
Figure 1 Growth in the number of seismic isolation structure ratings
02:41
2. 2. Issues of seismic control structure

Around the time when the bubble economy was brilliant, there was a lot of movement that seismic isolation was followed by active vibration control. However, it is difficult to actively control thousands of tons of buildings against severe earthquake motion, and after the Great Hanshin Earthquake, solid passive seismic control aimed at improving seismic safety has been used in the design of high-rise buildings. The number of cases of adopting is increasing. Some seismic isolated buildings have already been designed to be safe against Vmax = 100 cm / s level seismic motion, but most high-rise buildings are still designed against his Vmax = 50 cm / s level seismic motion. The reality is that it is.

3. 3. Issues of seismic isolation structure

There are various discussions and movements regarding the technical issues of seismic isolation structures, but I think we should be careful not to misunderstand the essentials.
For example, it has been pointed out that measures against vertical seismic motion are an issue for seismic isolation, but vertical seismic isolation should be avoided with the normal support form and the current seismic isolation effect.
In addition, increasing the surface pressure of the seismic isolation device (for example, Ïƒv = 200kg / cm2) is usually unnecessary in general buildings and is not preferable. It should be recognized that it reduces the deformation capacity of the appliance while giving the condition that the response deformation is large, cutting off the safety of the entire building.
Improving the safety of lightweight structures such as houses is an important social issue. Seismic isolation housing is being tackled by applying small laminated rubber, etc., but we are against setting the design seismic motion to a lower value due to the convenience of the equipment supplier.
We hope to contribute to the realization of a seismic isolated building that is safe and comfortable even against extremely severe earthquake motion without losing sight of the original purpose of the seismic isolation structure.
02:41
â–  Issues of seismic isolation building 2-How to design public seismic isolation building-

After experiencing the Great Hanshin Earthquake, seismic isolation structures have begun to be adopted in public buildings such as hospitals and government buildings. By August 1996, there were 13 hospitals that had been rated, including 4 public hospitals. There are also 6 public buildings that correspond to government buildings. Although it is still a small number among the total of about 300 buildings, it seems that the active efforts of local governments that seismic isolation structures should be adopted for public buildings are spreading nationwide.

1. 1. Design method for public seismic isolated buildings

The design of public facilities can be divided into the design and construction batch ordering method for general contractors and the ordering method that separates design and construction, even for seismic isolated buildings, but the latter can be said to be common for public facilities.
Since there are several methods of seismic isolation construction method and seismic isolation device, the orderer may want to avoid specifying the seismic isolation device in the design of public works projects that require competitive bidding. There are three possible design methods for this.
1. Specify only the performance and do not decide the device.
2. Design multiple devices for multiple devices.
3. Identify and design the equipment suitable for the building.

2. 2. Comparison of each design method

In the method of 1.2 above, for example, assuming that the restoring force characteristics of the seismic isolation device are bilinear, the support load, yield load, post-yield rigidity and its allowable error range are specified, and if this performance is satisfied, the seismic isolation device is used. Is anything. Although it is a method with a high degree of freedom as an ordering form, this does not design the most important seismic isolation device, and in reality, it ignores the characteristics of each seismic isolation device and sets the design level to bilinear for anything. It will be spread.
Then, the method of designing multiple ways for each device is 2. This is a waste of tax, with a number of designs that aren't actually adopted. No matter how careful the design is, the design cannot be said to be complete unless the seismic isolation device is specified. This pillar can be steel, RC or wooden. Center ratings and ministerial approvals for designs for which the main structural members have not been determined are also strange.
02:41
3. 3. The biggest problem of the device unspecified method

The method that does not specify the device in 1.2 above has an even greater fatal defect for seismic isolated buildings.
As I emphasized many times in this series, the safety performance of seismic isolated buildings depends on the deformation ability of the equipment. It is natural as a seismic isolation structure that it is safe for inputs of about Vmax = 50 cm / s. In reality, not a few seismic motions around Vmax = 100 cm / s have been observed, and it is most important for seismic isolated buildings to be able to adequately cope with such severe seismic motions (especially their deformation). It's a challenge.
If you do not specify the device and take the order form that "any device is acceptable as long as it satisfies only the specified specifications", the rest will be a cost competition. The cost of a seismic isolation device is as small as possible, and the thinner the rubber layer, the cheaper it is, but it is natural that such a device has a smaller deformation capacity. In the cost competition ordering method, it must be said that only the equipment with the lowest safety margin is selected and the most important safety performance that does not appear in the design table is cut off.

4. How to design a public seismic isolated building

The above method is indispensable to realize excellent public seismic isolation construction. A designer who is familiar with the characteristics and design conditions of a building should design the seismic isolation device that is most suitable for the building. Seismic isolation devices are the most important structural members in seismic isolation buildings. Not specifying it is a waiver of the design act, otherwise you are not qualified as a designer.
Considering the construction cost of the entire building, the cost of the seismic isolation device is only a small part. In the future, the number of manufacturers of equipment will increase, and it is possible that we will enter the market from overseas. The identification of the device is a different dimension from the manufacturer's specification. If you were caught before the construction of a competitive bid and cut off the most important safety, it would be "what was the seismic isolation structure adopted for?"
The safety of seismic isolated buildings depends on the design, which depends on the ideas of the client and the designer. I hope that excellent public seismic isolation buildings will be realized all over the country, and that their power will be fully demonstrated in the event of an upcoming earthquake.

â–  How to save an existing building

â—‹ = â–³ = Ã— = 1/3. Damage rate of 773 pre-earthquake buildings near JR Sannomiya in the Great Hanshin Earthquake. It is reported that â—‹ = no damage + minor = 34%, â–³ = medium damage + small damage = 38%, Ã— = collapse + major damage = 29%. It may be a good result considering the strength of the earthquake motion, but the battle of 1/3 of the dead is terrible. About 10% of new earthquake-resistant deaths (collapse + wreck) in the area.
It seems that there are about the same percentage of death groups nationwide. In December 1995, the "Act on Promotion of Earthquake-Resistant Repair of Buildings" was enforced, and improvement of earthquake resistance of existing buildings is required nationwide.

1. 1. Basic idea of â€‹â€‹seismic retrofitting

This law aims to raise existing buildings that do not meet current seismic standards to the same level as new seismic standards, that is, to prevent the building from collapsing due to severe seismic motion.
However, satisfying the new seismic resistance does not solve the seismic problem. As mentioned above, the current seismic design method cannot cover the safety of contents such as furniture and equipment, the maintenance of building functions, and the preservation of assets.

2. 2. Current status of seismic isolation retrofit

Seismic Isolation Retrofit, which renovates existing buildings with inferior seismic performance with seismic isolation structures, is the only place in the United States. The Salt Lake City Courthouse (Photo 1), which was the first application in the world, is too famous, but it is a particularly suitable method for renovating historic buildings with high cultural property value. 3. 3. Current status of vibration control retrofit

Seismic retrofitting with a seismic control structure started at the same time as seismic isolation retrofitting, but examples can be seen only recently after the 1989 Roma Preta (LP) earthquake in the United States and the Great Hanshin Earthquake in 1995 in Japan. became.

02:44
4. Prospects for seismic retrofitting technology

In conventional seismic retrofitting, the response acceleration is increased in order to increase the rigidity and strength. Careful consideration should be given to whether increasing the yield strength, which raises even the seismic response, really improves seismic performance from a comprehensive perspective.
Seismic control retrofit, which enhances damping performance, is suitable for buildings with relatively low rigidity and high deformation performance, such as steel structures and high-rise buildings, and its application examples will steadily increase in the future.
Seismic isolation retrofit is an extremely effective method for improving overall performance including the contents. However, the conventional method requires a large-scale construction, so it is difficult to apply it only to structures with high asset value.
For improving the seismic performance of general low-rise buildings, which occupy most of the structure, a relatively simple and economical method with a large response suppression effect is desired. Dynamic design has the technology to meet the demand, and we are also working on the development of new technology.
